[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: d9d032fd1efaa9d3[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability has been detected during fuzzing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the Apache POI library. The fuzzer identified an attempted connection to an [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal domain [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggered while processing an XSSF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExcel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m file [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough the `XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor` class. This security issue is classified[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mas medium severity and indicates that untrusted data from the input file is being [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mused to initiate network connections, potentially leading to data exfiltration or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexposure of internal services.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m vulnerability detected [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the Jazzer fuzzer's security sanitizer. SSRF vulnerabilities occur when an [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplication fetches remote resources based on user-supplied data without proper [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation, allowing attackers to make the server perform arbitrary network [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequests.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is triggered during XML parsing operations within the Apache POI [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibrary's XSSF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExcel file format[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m processing pipeline. Specifically, the stack [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrace shows the following sequence:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer invokes `[0m[1;35mPOIXSSFFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which processes [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted Excel file input[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. This calls `[0m[1;35mPOIFuzzer.checkExtractor[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which attempts to extract text from the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdocument[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The extraction process invokes `[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` methods[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. During XML parsing via `[0m[1;35mSAXParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, the XML entity scanner [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mXMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl.scanEntityReference[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m encounters an entity [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. The XML entity manager attempts to resolve this reference by calling [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLEntityManager.startEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35msetupCurrentEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. This triggers an HTTP connection attempt to the external domain [0m[32m"jazze.com:80"[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrough `[0m[1;35mHttpURLConnection.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. The Jazzer SSRF sanitizer intercepts the socket connection attempt in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrfSocket[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and raises the security exception[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability appears to stem from XML External Entity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXXE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m processing, where [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious XML content within the Excel file contains entity references pointing to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal URLs. The XML parser attempts to resolve these entities by making outbound[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTTP connections without proper validation or restriction.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKey areas of the codebase that should be investigated for a holistic understanding:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m299[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m316[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Examine how this class [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitializes and configures the SAX parser, particularly whether it disables [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entity resolution[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **XML Parser Configuration**: Review the SAXParser configuration used throughout[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe POI XSSF package to determine if external entity processing is properly [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabled[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **XMLEntityManager**: Investigate how entity references are resolved and whether[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthere are any validation mechanisms for external entities[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **POI Security Configuration**: Check if there are global security settings or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecommended configurations for preventing XXE/SSRF attacks when processing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted Office documents[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Related Extractors**: Examine other extractor classes in the POI library to [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetermine if this vulnerability is present in other document format handlers[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis finding is particularly concerning because Office document processing is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommonly performed on user-uploaded files in enterprise applications, making SSRF [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerabilities in document parsers a significant security risk. The vulnerability [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcould allow attackers to scan internal networks, access internal services, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexfiltrate sensitive data, or perform denial-of-service attacks against external [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msystems.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<issue>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m539[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39minAppVersion[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m540[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.append[0m[1;39m([0m[39mch, start, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Analysis of the Vulnerability[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe SSRF vulnerability exists in the [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m, where it [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreates an unsecured SAXParser using [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` without any security configuration.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis parser will attempt to resolve external entities in XML, leading to XXE/SSRF [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacks.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The method bypasses Apache POI's established security infrastructure [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLHelper [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutility[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- It directly uses SAXParserFactory without disabling external entity resolution[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is inconsistent with the secure pattern used elsewhere in the same class [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m251[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key Finding:**[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe class already has access to securely-parsed extended properties through its [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`properties` field [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPOIXMLProperties instance[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but reimplements XML parsing for [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperformance optimization, introducing the vulnerability.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Recommended Fix Strategy[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Use [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMinimal Change - RECOMMENDED[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the insecure SAXParser creation with [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to apply the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msame security configuration used throughout the codebase.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes Required:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- File: [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`poi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m.java`[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Method: `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStringBuilder text[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at lines [0m[1;36m308[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m320[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Replace line [0m[1;36m315[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m316[0m[39m:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m OLD [0m[1;39m([0m[39mVULNERABLE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   With:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```java[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m NEW [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSECURE[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   XMLReader xmlReader = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mxmlReader.setContentHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mxmlReader.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Update imports if necessary [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLReader and InputSource are already imported at [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m65[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m63[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Works:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.newXMLReader[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` creates an XMLReader with all security features [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menabled:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Disables DOCTYPE declarations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFEATURE_DISALLOW_DOCTYPE_DECL[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Disables external entities [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Disables external DTD loading [0m[1;39m([0m[39mFEATURE_LOAD_EXTERNAL_DTD[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Sets entity resolver to ignore entities[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Limits entity expansion to [0m[1;36m1[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is the exact same pattern used in `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method at line [0m[1;36m251[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains the same performance characteristics [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSAX event-based parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to ExtendedPropertiesHandler needed[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Minimal code changes with maximum security impact[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Use POIXMLProperties API [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMore Comprehensive[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the entire [0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method to use the already-securely-parsed [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPOIXMLProperties object instead of re-parsing XML.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReplace the entire `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m308[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m320[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate void [0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStringBuilder text[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mappendProp.accept[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Company"[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mext.getCompany[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Add other properties as needed[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Works:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Uses the already-securely-parsed POIXMLProperties object [0m[1;39m([0m[39mloaded at line [0m[1;36m96[0m[39m with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure XML parsing[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates all XML parsing from this method[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- More maintainable and consistent with the rest of the POI codebase[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No XXE/SSRF risk since no XML parsing occurs[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ExtendedPropertiesHandler class [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m485[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m543[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can be removed entirely[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m is Recommended:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Minimal disruption**: Changes only [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m lines of code[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Consistent pattern**: Matches the secure pattern used in `[0m[1;35mprocessSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m251[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `[0m[1;35mReadOnlySharedStringsTable.readFrom[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m195[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Preserves functionality**: ExtendedPropertiesHandler continues to work without [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodification[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Performance**: Maintains SAX event-based parsing efficiency[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Security**: Applies all XXE protections from XMLHelper utility[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Testing**: Less risk of breaking existing tests since behavior is preserved[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m is Also Valid:**[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Eliminates redundancy**: Removes duplicate XML parsing logic[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **More maintainable**: Uses standard POI APIs[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Cleaner code**: Removes ExtendedPropertiesHandler inner class [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m60[0m[39m lines[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Future-proof**: Any updates to ExtendedProperties API automatically benefit [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis code[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Risks and Mitigation:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Risk**: Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m might produce slightly different text output format[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - **Mitigation**: Carefully match the formatting logic from [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Risk**: Performance impact of loading full POIXMLProperties vs SAX parsing[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - **Mitigation**: POIXMLProperties is already loaded at line [0m[1;36m96[0m[39m, so Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m has [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mno additional overhead[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Risk**: Breaking existing tests that verify exact text output[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - **Mitigation**: Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m maintains exact same output; Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m requires test [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidation[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
